File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml\continue_training.py
1: import torch
2: import torch.nn as nn
3: import torch.optim as optim
4: import numpy as np
5: import chess
6: from nn_parse_pgn import process_pgn_files  # Import the function to process PGN files
7: 
8: print("Starting program...")
9: 
10: class ChessNet(nn.Module):
11:     def __init__(self):
12:         super(ChessNet, self).__init__()
13:         self.fc1 = nn.Linear(768, 128)  # Input size is 768 (binary matrix size)
14:         self.fc2 = nn.Linear(128, 64)
15:         self.fc3 = nn.Linear(64, 64)  # Output size is 64 (one-hot encoding size)
16: 
17:     def forward(self, x):
18:         x = torch.relu(self.fc1(x))
19:         x = torch.relu(self.fc2(x))
20:         x = self.fc3(x)
21:         return x
22: 
23: # Load the pre-trained model
24: model = ChessNet()
25: model.load_state_dict(torch.load("chess_model.pth"))
26: 
27: print("Pre-trained model loaded...")
28: 
29: # Convert UCI move to one-hot encoding
30: def uci_to_one_hot(move):
31:     start_square = ord(move[0]) - ord('a') + (8 - int(move[1])) * 8
32:     end_square = ord(move[2]) - ord('a') + (8 - int(move[3])) * 8
33:     return start_square, end_square
34: 
35: print("UCI -> One hot encoding conversion defined...")
36: 
37: # Load data generator
38: data_generator = process_pgn_files("../data")
39: 
40: print("Data generator created...")
41: 
42: # Create loss function and optimizer
43: criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
44: optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)
45: 
46: print("Beginning training...")
47: 
48: # Train the model
49: num_epochs = 1  # Changed to 1 for testing, was 10
50: for epoch in range(num_epochs):
51:     print(f"Epoch [{epoch+1}/{num_epochs}]")
52:     num_batches = 0
53:     total_loss = 0
54:     move_counter = 0
55:     for board, move in data_generator:
56:         print(f"{epoch} - {move_counter} - Starting forward pass...")
57:         # Convert UCI board position to binary matrix
58:         def uci_to_binary(board):
59:             binary_matrix = np.zeros((64, 12), dtype=np.uint8)
60:             piece_indices = {'p': 0, 'P': 1, 'n': 2, 'N': 3, 'b': 4, 'B': 5, 'r': 6, 'R': 7, 'q': 8, 'Q': 9, 'k': 10, 'K': 11}
61:             for square, piece in board.piece_map().items():
62:                 if piece.piece_type != chess.PAWN:
63:                     binary_matrix[square][piece_indices[piece.symbol().lower()]] = 1
64:             return binary_matrix.flatten()
65:         X_data = uci_to_binary(chess.Board(board))
66:         X_data = torch.tensor(X_data, dtype=torch.float32).unsqueeze(0)  # Add batch dimension
67:         # Convert UCI move to one-hot encoding
68:         y_data = uci_to_one_hot(move)
69:         y_data = torch.tensor(y_data[1], dtype=torch.long).unsqueeze(0)  # Add batch dimension
70:         print(f"{epoch} - {move_counter} - Starting backpropagation...")
71:         optimizer.zero_grad()
72:         outputs = model(X_data)
73:         loss = criterion(outputs, y_data)
74:         loss.backward()
75:         optimizer.step()
76:         num_batches += 1
77:         total_loss += loss.item()
78:         move_counter += 1
79:     average_loss = total_loss / num_batches
80:     print(f"  Average Loss: {average_loss:.4f}")
81: 
82: # Save the updated model
83: torch.save(model.state_dict(), "chess_model.pth")
84: 
85: print("Training completed. Updated model saved.")
86: 


File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml\make_prediction.py
1: import torch
2: import torch.nn as nn
3: import numpy as np
4: import chess
5: from nn_parse_pgn import process_pgn_files  # Import the function to process PGN files
6: 
7: print("Starting program...")
8: 
9: class ChessNet(nn.Module):
10:     def __init__(self):
11:         super(ChessNet, self).__init__()
12:         self.fc1 = nn.Linear(768, 128)  # Input size is 768 (binary matrix size)
13:         self.fc2 = nn.Linear(128, 64)
14:         self.fc3 = nn.Linear(64, 64)  # Output size is 64 (one-hot encoding size)
15: 
16:     def forward(self, x):
17:         x = torch.relu(self.fc1(x))
18:         x = torch.relu(self.fc2(x))
19:         x = self.fc3(x)
20:         return x
21: 
22: # Load the pre-trained model
23: model = ChessNet()
24: model.load_state_dict(torch.load("chess_model.pth"))
25: 
26: print("ChessNet defined and pre-trained model loaded...")
27: 
28: def index_to_algebraic(index):
29:     start_square = index // 64
30:     end_square = index % 64
31:     start_square_coords = chess.square_name(start_square)
32:     end_square_coords = chess.square_name(end_square)
33:     return start_square_coords + end_square_coords
34: 
35: # Convert UCI move to one-hot encoding
36: def uci_to_one_hot(move):
37:     start_square = ord(move[0]) - ord('a') + (8 - int(move[1])) * 8
38:     end_square = ord(move[2]) - ord('a') + (8 - int(move[3])) * 8
39:     return start_square, end_square
40: 
41: print("UCI -> One hot encoding conversion defined...")
42: 
43: # Get user input for board representation in UCI format
44: board_position = input("Enter the board position in UCI format: ")
45: 
46: # Convert UCI board position to binary matrix
47: def uci_to_binary(board):
48:     binary_matrix = np.zeros((64, 12), dtype=np.uint8)
49:     piece_indices = {'p': 0, 'P': 1, 'n': 2, 'N': 3, 'b': 4, 'B': 5, 'r': 6, 'R': 7, 'q': 8, 'Q': 9, 'k': 10, 'K': 11}
50:     for square, piece in board.piece_map().items():
51:         if piece.piece_type != chess.PAWN:
52:             binary_matrix[square][piece_indices[piece.symbol().lower()]] = 1
53:     return binary_matrix.flatten()
54: 
55: X_data = uci_to_binary(chess.Board(board_position))
56: X_data = torch.tensor(X_data, dtype=torch.float32).unsqueeze(0)  # Add batch dimension
57: 
58: # Make predictions
59: outputs = model(X_data)
60: predicted_move_index = torch.argmax(outputs)
61: print(f"Predicted Move Index: {predicted_move_index}")
62: 
63: predicted_move = index_to_algebraic(predicted_move_index.item())
64: print(f"Predicted Move: {predicted_move}")
65: 
66: print("Prediction process completed.")
67:

File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml\nn.py
1: import torch
2: import torch.nn as nn
3: import torch.optim as optim
4: import numpy as np
5: from nn_parse_pgn import process_pgn_files  # Import the function to process PGN files
6: 
7: class ChessNet(nn.Module):
8:     def __init__(self):
9:         super(ChessNet, self).__init__()
10:         self.fc1 = nn.Linear(64, 128)  # Input size is 64 (chess board squares)
11:         self.fc2 = nn.Linear(128, 64)
12:         self.fc3 = nn.Linear(64, 3)  # Output size is 3 (win/loss/draw)
13: 
14:     def forward(self, x):
15:         x = torch.relu(self.fc1(x))
16:         x = torch.relu(self.fc2(x))
17:         x = self.fc3(x)
18:         return x
19: 
20: # Prepare data for training using nn_parse_pgn.py
21: X_data, y_data = process_pgn_files("../data")
22: X_data = np.array(X_data)
23: y_data = np.array(y_data)
24: 
25: # Convert data to PyTorch tensors
26: print(X_data.shape)
27: inputs = torch.tensor(X_data, dtype=torch.float32)
28: labels = torch.tensor(y_data, dtype=torch.long)
29: 
30: # Create model, loss function, and optimizer
31: model = ChessNet()
32: criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
33: optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)
34: 
35: # Train the model
36: num_epochs = 10
37: batch_size = 32
38: num_samples = len(inputs)
39: for epoch in range(num_epochs):
40:     for i in range(0, num_samples, batch_size):
41:         optimizer.zero_grad()
42:         batch_inputs = inputs[i:i+batch_size]
43:         batch_labels = labels[i:i+batch_size]
44:         outputs = model(batch_inputs)
45:         loss = criterion(outputs, batch_labels)
46:         loss.backward()
47:         optimizer.step()
48:     print(f"Epoch [{epoch+1}/{num_epochs}], Loss: {loss.item():.4f}")
49: 
50: # Save the trained model
51: torch.save(model.state_dict(), "chess_model.pth")
52: 


File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml\nn3.py
1: import torch
2: import torch.nn as nn
3: import torch.optim as optim
4: import numpy as np
5: from nn_parse_pgn import process_pgn_files  # Import the function to process PGN files
6: import chess
7: 
8: class ChessNet(nn.Module):
9:     def __init__(self):
10:         super(ChessNet, self).__init__()
11:         self.fc1 = nn.Linear(64, 128)  # Input size is 64 (chess board squares)
12:         self.fc2 = nn.Linear(128, 64)
13:         self.fc3 = nn.Linear(64, 3)  # Output size is 3 (win/loss/draw)
14: 
15:     def forward(self, x):
16:         x = torch.relu(self.fc1(x))
17:         x = torch.relu(self.fc2(x))
18:         x = self.fc3(x)
19:         return x
20: 
21: def uci_to_binary(board):
22:     # Create binary matrix
23:     binary_matrix = np.zeros((64, 12), dtype=np.uint8)
24:     # Map pieces to indices
25:     piece_indices = {
26:         'p': 0, 'P': 1, 'n': 2, 'N': 3, 'b': 4, 'B': 5,
27:         'r': 6, 'R': 7, 'q': 8, 'Q': 9, 'k': 10, 'K': 11
28:     }
29:     # Populate binary matrix
30:     for square, piece in board.piece_map().items():
31:         if piece.piece_type != chess.PAWN:
32:             binary_matrix[square][piece_indices[piece.symbol().lower()]] = 1
33:     return binary_matrix.flatten()
34: 
35: # Convert UCI move to one-hot encoding
36: def uci_to_one_hot(move):
37:     start_square = ord(move[0]) - ord('a') + (8 - int(move[1])) * 8
38:     end_square = ord(move[2]) - ord('a') + (8 - int(move[3])) * 8
39:     return start_square, end_square
40: 
41: # Prepare data for training using nn_parse_pgn.py
42: X_data, y_data = process_pgn_files("../data")
43: 
44: # Convert data to numpy arrays
45: X_data = np.array(X_data)
46: y_data = np.array(y_data)
47: 
48: # Convert UCI board positions to binary matrices
49: X_data = np.array([uci_to_binary(chess.Board(position)) for position in X_data])
50: 
51: # Convert UCI moves to one-hot encoding
52: y_data = np.array([uci_to_one_hot(move) for move in y_data])
53: 
54: # Convert data to PyTorch tensors
55: inputs = torch.tensor(X_data, dtype=torch.float32)
56: labels = torch.tensor(y_data, dtype=torch.long)
57: 
58: # Print the shape of X_data
59: print(X_data.shape)
60: 
61: # Create model, loss function, and optimizer
62: model = ChessNet()
63: criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
64: optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)
65: 
66: # Train the model
67: num_epochs = 10
68: batch_size = 32
69: num_samples = len(inputs)
70: for epoch in range(num_epochs):
71:     for i in range(0, num_samples, batch_size):
72:         optimizer.zero_grad()
73:         batch_inputs = inputs[i:i+batch_size]
74:         batch_labels = labels[i:i+batch_size]
75:         outputs = model(batch_inputs)
76:         loss = criterion(outputs, batch_labels)
77:         loss.backward()
78:         optimizer.step()
79:     print(f"Epoch [{epoch+1}/{num_epochs}], Loss: {loss.item():.4f}")
80: 
81: # Save the trained model
82: torch.save(model.state_dict(), "chess_model.pth")

49:     num_batches = 0

52:     for board, move in data_generator:
53:         print(f"{epoch} - {move_counter} - Starting forward pass...")
54:         # Convert UCI board position to binary matrix
55:         def uci_to_binary(board):
56:             binary_matrix = np.zeros((64, 12), dtype=np.uint8)
57:             piece_indices = {'p': 0, 'P': 1, 'n': 2, 'N': 3, 'b': 4, 'B': 5, 'r': 6, 'R': 7, 'q': 8, 'Q': 9, 'k': 10, 'K': 11}

64:         # Convert UCI move to one-hot encoding

66:         y_data = torch.tensor(y_data[1], dtype=torch.long).unsqueeze(0)  # Add batch dimension
67:         print(f"{epoch} - {move_counter} - Starting backpropagation...")
68:         optimizer.zero_grad()
69:         outputs = model(X_data)
70:         loss = criterion(outputs, y_data)
71:         loss.backward()
72:         optimizer.step()
73:         num_batches += 1
74:         total_loss += loss.item()
75:     average_loss = total_loss / num_batches
76:     print(f"  Average Loss: {average_loss:.4f}")
77:

79: torch.save(model.state_dict(), "chess_model.pth")


File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml\nn_parse_pgn.py
1: import os
2: import chess.pgn
3: import numpy as np
4: 
5: # Specify the training_directory containing training data
6: training_directory = "../data"
7: 
8: def encode_board_to_uci(board):
9:     return board.fen()
10: 
11: def encode_move_to_uci(move):
12:     return move.uci()
13: 
14: def process_pgn_files(training_directory):
15:     # Iterate over each file in the directory
16:     for filename in os.listdir(training_directory):
17:         if filename.endswith(".pgn"):  # Check if the file is a PGN file
18:             filepath = os.path.join(training_directory, filename)
19: 
20:             # Open the PGN file
21:             with open(filepath) as pgn_file:
22:                 # Iterate over each game in the PGN file
23:                 while True:
24:                     # Read the game from the PGN file
25:                     game = chess.pgn.read_game(pgn_file)
26: 
27:                     # Check if there are no more games in the file
28:                     if game is None:
29:                         break
30: 
31:                     # Iterate over each move in the game
32:                     board = game.board()
33:                     for move in game.mainline_moves():
34:                         # Encode the board representation to UCI format
35:                         encoded_board = encode_board_to_uci(board)
36:                         # Encode the move to UCI format
37:                         encoded_move = encode_move_to_uci(move)
38:                         # Make the move on the board for the next iteration
39:                         board.push(move)
40:                         # Yield the encoded board and move
41:                         print (encoded_board)
42:                         yield encoded_board, encoded_move
43: 
44:

46: #     print(encoded_board)

File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml\testing_pytorch_pgn.py
1: import torch
2: import torch.nn as nn
3: import torch.optim as optim
4: import torch.nn.functional as F
5: from torch.utils.data import DataLoader
6: from torch.utils.data import Dataset
7: import chess  # Library for handling chess data
8: import chess.pgn  # Module for reading PGN files
9: import numpy as np
10: from chess import square
11: 
12: # Load PGN file
13: pgn_file = open(r"C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\data\bobby1.pgn")
14: 
15: # Create lists to store game data
16: X_train = []
17: y_train = []
18: 
19: # Assuming an 8x8x12 board representation
20: input_features = 8 * 8 * 12
21: 
22: num_epochs = 100
23: 
24: def create_board_representation(game, move):
25:     """Creates a numerical representation of the board state."""
26:     board = game.board()
27:     board_array = np.zeros((8, 8, 12), dtype=np.float32)  # Array for piece positions
28: 
29:     # Map pieces to numerical values
30:     piece_map = {"P": 1, "N": 2, "B": 3, "R": 4, "Q": 5, "K": 6, "p": -1, "n": -2, "b": -3, "r": -4, "q": -5, "k": -6}
31: 
32:     for rank in range(8):
33:         for file in range(8):
34:             piece = board.piece_at(square(rank, file))
35:             if piece:
36:                 board_array[rank, file, piece_map[piece.symbol().upper()]] = 1.0
37: 
38:     return board_array.flatten()  # Flatten to a 1D array
39: 
40: def get_outcome(game):
41:     """Extracts the game outcome from the PGN."""
42:     root_node = game.root()  # Access the root node
43:     result = root_node.headers["Result"]
44:     if result == "1-0":
45:         return 1  # White win
46:     elif result == "0-1":
47:         return 0  # Black win
48:     else:
49:         return 0.5  # Draw
50: 
51: for game in chess.pgn.read_game(pgn_file):
52:     for move in game.mainline_moves():
53:         board_representation = create_board_representation(game, move)
54:         outcome = get_outcome(game)  # Extract the outcome
55: 
56:         X_train.append(board_representation)
57:         y_train.append(outcome)  # Append both board and outcome
58: 
59: # Convert data to PyTorch tensors
60: X_train = np.array(X_train)
61: X_train = torch.tensor(X_train, dtype=torch.float32)
62: y_train = np.array(y_train)
63: y_train = torch.tensor(y_train, dtype=torch.int64)  # Assuming integer labels for outcomes
64: 
65: class ChessNet(nn.Module):
66:     def __init__(self):
67:         super().__init__()
68:         self.fc1 = nn.Linear(input_features, 128)
69:         self.fc2 = nn.Linear(128, 64)
70:         # Output layer for move probabilities (64 squares)
71:         self.fc3 = nn.Linear(64, 64)
72: 
73:     def forward(self, x):
74:         x = torch.flatten(x, 1)  # Flatten input for linear layers
75:         x = F.relu(self.fc1(x))
76:         x = F.relu(self.fc2(x))
77:         # Output move probabilities
78:         x = F.softmax(self.fc3(x), dim=1)
79:         return x
80: 
81: model = ChessNet()
82: criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()  # Adjust loss function if needed
83: optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)
84: 
85: # Training loop
86: for epoch in range(num_epochs):
87:     # Forward pass
88:     outputs = model(X_train)
89:     loss = criterion(outputs, y_train)
90: 
91:     # Backward pass and optimization
92:     optimizer.zero_grad()
93:     loss.backward()
94:     optimizer.step()
95: 
96:     # Print training progress
97:     print(f"Epoch [{epoch+1}/{num_epochs}], Loss: {loss.item():.4f}")
98: 
99: class ChessDataset(Dataset):
100:     def __init__(self, data):
101:         # Load and preprocess your chess data here
102:         self.data = data
103: 
104: def __len__(self):
105:     # Returns the total number of samples in the dataset
106:     return len(self.data)
107: 
108: def __getitem__(self, idx):
109:     # Retrieves a single sample (board representation, move) by index
110:     board_rep, move = self.data[idx]
111:     # Preprocess sample if needed (e.g., convert to tensors)
112:     return board_rep, move
113: 
114: train_loader = DataLoader(
115:     dataset=your_chess_dataset,  # Replace with your dataset object
116:     batch_size=32,  # Adjust batch size as needed
117:     shuffle=True  # Shuffle data for better training
118: )
119: 
120: # In the training loop:
121: for epoch in range(num_epochs):
122:     for i, (X_train_batch, y_train_batch) in enumerate(train_loader):
123: 		  # Forward propogation
124:         model.train()  # Set model to training mode
125:         output = model(X_train_batch)
126:         loss = criterion(output, y_train_batch) # Calculate loss based on move predictions and actual moves
127: 		  # Backward propogation
128:         optimizer.zero_grad()
129:         loss.backward()
130:         optimizer.step()
131: 
132:     # Print training progress

File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/python\count_lines.py
1: import os
2: 
3: def count_lines(file_path):
4:     with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
5:         return sum(1 for line in file if line.strip() and not line.strip().startswith('#'))
6: 
7: def count_lines_in_directory(directory):
8:     total_lines = 0
9:     for root, dirs, files in os.walk(directory):
10:         for file in files:
11:             file_path = os.path.join(root, file)
12:             total_lines += count_lines(file_path)
13:     return total_lines
14: 
15: if __name__ == "__main__":
16:     directory = input("Enter directory path: ")
17:     lines_of_code = count_lines_in_directory(directory)
18:     print(f"Total lines of executable code: {lines_of_code}")


File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/python\get_evaluation.py
1: from stockfish import Stockfish
2: 
3: def get_board_evaluation(fen_string):
4: 
5:   # Set up Stockfish engine (replace with your engine path if needed)
6:   engine = Stockfish(r"C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\stockfish\stockfish-windows-x86-64-avx2.exe")
7: 
8:   engine.set_fen_position(fen_string)
9:   evaluation = engine.get_evaluation()
10: 
11:   if evaluation["type"] == "cp":
12:     return f"{evaluation['value'] / 100}?{evaluation['type']}"
13:   elif evaluation["type"] == "mate":
14:     return f"{evaluation['value']}?{evaluation['type']}"
15:   else:

File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/python\get_stats.py
1: from stockfish import Stockfish
2: 
3: def get_game_stats(fen_string):
4:   engine = Stockfish(r"C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\stockfish\stockfish-windows-x86-64-avx2.exe")
5:   engine.set_depth(5)
6:   engine.set_elo_rating(800)
7: 
8:   engine.set_fen_position(fen_string)
9: 
10:   move = engine.get_best_move()
11: 
12:   evaluation = engine.get_evaluation()
13: 
14:   if evaluation["type"] == "cp":
15:     game_eval = f"{evaluation['value'] / 100}?{evaluation['type']}"
16:   elif evaluation["type"] == "mate":
17:     game_eval = f"{evaluation['value']}?{evaluation['type']}"
18: 
19:   return f"{move}&{game_eval}"

File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/python\parse_evaluation.cpp
1: #include <iostream>
2: #include <sstream>
3: #include <string>
4: #include <cmath>
5: 
6: struct evaluation {
7: 	double value; // Represents advantage if cp, or moves until mate if mate
8: 	int winning;  // 1 - white, 2 - black
9: 	int status;   // 1 - cp, 2 - mate
10: };
11: 
12: int main(void) {
13: 
14: 	evaluation eval;
15: 	std::string eval_string = "-1.00?mate";
16: 
17: 	int separator = eval_string.find('?');
18: 
19: 	// Get the game state
20: 	eval.status = (eval_string.substr(separator + 1) == "cp") ? 1 : 2;
21: 
22:    // Get the evaluation value
23:    std::stringstream(eval_string.substr(0, separator)) >> eval.value;
24: 
25: 	// Determine who is winning
26: 	eval.winning = eval.value >= 0 ? 1 : 2;
27: 
28: 	// After determining who is winning, now can take abs value of value
29:    eval.value = std::abs(eval.value);
30: 
31: 	std::cout << "value: " << eval.value << std::endl;
32: 	std::cout << "status (1 - cp, 2 - mate): " << eval.status << std::endl;
33:    std::cout << "winning: " << eval.winning << std::endl;
34: 
35: 	return 0;
36: }

104: void BoardScreen::moveCompleted(QString algebraic, int winning, int evaluation)
105: {
106:     // Update move bank
107:     if (this->ui->lbl_moveDisplay->text().isEmpty()) {
108:         this->setMovesLabel(algebraic);
109:         return;
110:     }
111: 
112:     QString currentText = this->getMovesLabel();
113:     currentText = currentText + ", " + algebraic;
114:     this->setMovesLabel(currentText);
115: 
116:     // Update evaluation bar
117:     int value = winning == 1 ? evaluation : (0 - evaluation);
118:     evalBar->setEvaluation(value);
119: 
120:     return;
121: }

20: 
21: class BoardScreen : public QMainWindow
22: {
23:     Q_OBJECT
24: 
25: public:
26:     explicit BoardScreen(QWidget *parent = nullptr);
27:     ~BoardScreen();
28:     void setMovesLabel(QString updatedString);
29:     QString getMovesLabel();
30: 
31: Q_SIGNALS:
32:     void boardScreenClosed();
33:     void blackToPlay();
34: 
35: private:
36:     Ui::BoardScreen *ui;
37:     QWidget *parentForm;
38:     Config *config;
39:     EvaluationBar *evalBar;
40:     void setMascot();
41: 
42:     struct evaluation {
43:         double value = 0; // Represents advantage if cp, or moves until mate if mate
44:         int winning = 0;  // 1 - white, 2 - black
45:         int status = 0;   // 1 - cp, 2 - mate
46:     };
47: 
48: private Q_SLOTS:
49:     void on_btn_closeWindow_clicked();
50:     void moveCompleted(QString algebraic, int winning, int evaluation); // See evaluation struct in ChessBoard.h for details on winning and evaluation
51:     void switchMascot(int status);
52:     void game_over(QString notification);
53: };
54: 
55: #endif // BOARDSCREEN_H

98:           <string>&lt;!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC &quot;-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0//EN&quot; &quot;http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/strict.dtd&quot;&gt;
99: &lt;html&gt;&lt;head&gt;&lt;meta name=&quot;qrichtext&quot; content=&quot;1&quot; /&gt;&lt;meta charset=&quot;utf-8&quot; /&gt;&lt;title&gt;Chess Rules&lt;/title&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;
100: p, li { white-space: pre-wrap; }
101: &lt;/style&gt;&lt;/head&gt;&lt;body style=&quot; font-family:'Arial'; font-size:12pt; font-weight:400; font-style:normal;&quot;&gt;
102: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console'; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;The Board and Pieces &lt;/span&gt;     &lt;/p&gt;
103: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot;&gt;Chess is played on a checkered board with 64 squares arranged in an 8x8 grid. Each square alternates in color,light and dark. &lt;/span&gt;     &lt;/p&gt;
104: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot;&gt;Each player starts with 16 pieces: 8 pawns,2 rooks,2 knights,2 bishops,1 queen,and 1 king. The pieces are placed on the starting squares at the opposite ends of the board. Pawns are positioned in front,with the other pieces lined up behind them. The queen sits on the square that matches her color (white on white, black on black). &lt;/span&gt;     &lt;/p&gt;
105: &lt;h2 style=&quot; margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console'; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;How Pieces Move &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;     &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
106: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot;&gt;Each chess piece has a unique way of moving. A piece can move to an empty square or capture an opponent's piece by landing on its square. Pieces cannot jump over other pieces (except the knight). &lt;/span&gt;     &lt;/p&gt;
107: &lt;ul style=&quot;margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; -qt-list-indent: 1;&quot;&gt;&lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Pawn:&lt;/span&gt;Pawns move forward one square at a time, except for their first move where they can move one or two squares. They capture diagonally and cannot move backward. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
108: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Rook:&lt;/span&gt;Rooks move any number of squares horizontally or vertically. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
109: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Bishop:&lt;/span&gt;Bishops move any number of squares diagonally. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
110: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Knight:&lt;/span&gt;Knights move in an &amp;quot; L&amp;quot; shape, two squares in one direction and then one square perpendicularly. They are the only piece that can jump over other pieces. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
111: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Queen:&lt;/span&gt;The queen combines the moves of the rook and bishop, moving any number of squares in any direction (horizontally, vertically, or diagonally). &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
112: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;King:&lt;/span&gt;The king moves one square in any direction (horizontal, vertical, or diagonal). The king's safety is paramount, and it cannot move into a position where it would be captured (check). &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                        &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;
113: &lt;h2 style=&quot; margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console'; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Special Moves &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;     &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
114: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot;&gt;Chess has two special moves: castling and en passant. &lt;/span&gt;     &lt;/p&gt;
115: &lt;ul style=&quot;margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; -qt-list-indent: 1;&quot;&gt;&lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Castling:&lt;/span&gt;This involves moving the king and a rook together under certain conditions. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
116: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;En passant:&lt;/span&gt;This is a special pawn capture that can occur immediately after an opponent's pawn moves two squares from its starting position. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                        &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;
117: &lt;h2 style=&quot; margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console'; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Winning the Game &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;     &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
118: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot;&gt;The objective of chess is to checkmate your opponent's king. Checkmate occurs when the king is under immediate threat of capture (check) and has no legal move to escape. &lt;/span&gt;     &lt;/p&gt;
119: &lt;h2 style=&quot; margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console'; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Other Important Rules &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;     &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
120: &lt;ul style=&quot;margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; -qt-list-indent: 1;&quot;&gt;&lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;Players take turns, with white always moving first. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
121: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;A pawn that reaches the other side of the board can be promoted to another piece (queen, rook, bishop, or knight). &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
122: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;The game can also end in a stalemate, where a player is not in check but has no legal move due to their own pieces blocking their king's movement. In this case, the game is a draw. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                        &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;
123: &lt;p style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:15px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console'; font-size:x-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Chess Appendix&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-size:xx-large; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;    &lt;/p&gt;
124: &lt;ul style=&quot;margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; -qt-list-indent: 1;&quot;&gt;&lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Checkmate:&lt;/span&gt;When the king is in a position to be captured and cannot escape capture, thus ending the game. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
125: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Check:&lt;/span&gt;When a player's king is under immediate threat of capture by an opponent' s piece. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
126: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Stalemate:&lt;/span&gt;A situation in which a player's king is not in check, but they have no legal moves to make, resulting in a draw. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
127: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Castling:&lt;/span&gt;A special move involving the king and one of the rooks, where the king moves two squares towards a rook, and that rook moves to the square next to the king. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
128: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;En passant:&lt;/span&gt;A special pawn capture that can occur when a pawn moves two squares forward from its starting position and lands next to an opponent's pawn, allowing that opponent' s pawn to capture it as if it had only moved one square. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
129: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Pawn promotion:&lt;/span&gt;When a pawn reaches the opposite side of the board, it can be promoted to any other piece (except a king). &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
130: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Algebraic notation:&lt;/span&gt;The system used to record moves in chess, where each square is identified by a unique coordinate. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
131: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Tactics:&lt;/span&gt;Short-term sequences of moves used to achieve specific objectives, such as capturing pieces or creating threats. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
132: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Strategy:&lt;/span&gt;Long-term plans and positional considerations aimed at gaining an advantage over the opponent. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
133: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Development:&lt;/span&gt;The process of bringing pieces into play, usually by moving them from their initial positions to more active squares. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
134: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Control of the center:&lt;/span&gt;Establishing dominance over the central squares of the board, which provides greater mobility for pieces and better control of the game. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
135: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Open file:&lt;/span&gt;A column on the chessboard that contains no pawns of either color, allowing rooks to move freely along it. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
136: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Pin:&lt;/span&gt;When a piece is unable to move because it would expose a more valuable piece behind it to capture. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
137: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Fork:&lt;/span&gt;A tactic in which one piece simultaneously attacks two or more opponent pieces. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
138: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Skewer:&lt;/span&gt;A tactical maneuver where a valuable piece is attacked and forced to move, exposing a less valuable piece behind it to capture. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
139: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Zugzwang:&lt;/span&gt;A situation in which any move a player makes weakens their position, often leading to a disadvantage or loss. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
140: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Tempo:&lt;/span&gt;The concept of time or initiative in chess, often gained by forcing the opponent to make moves they do not want to make. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
141: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Sacrifice:&lt;/span&gt;Intentionally giving up material (usually a piece) to gain a positional or tactical advantage. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
142: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Initiative:&lt;/span&gt;Having control over the course of the game and dictating the flow of play. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;                    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
143: &lt;li style=&quot; font-family:'Lucida Console';&quot; style=&quot; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot; font-weight:700;&quot;&gt;Endgame:&lt;/span&gt;The stage of the game where there are few pieces left on the board, requiring precise calculation and technique to convert advantages into a win. &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;            &lt;/span&gt; &lt;span style=&quot; font-family:'Arial';&quot;&gt;    &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/body&gt;&lt;/html&gt;</string>
144:          </property>
145:         </widget>
146:        </item>

15:     ui(new Ui::SettingsScreen)

33: void SettingsScreen::fillComboBoxes()
34: {
35:     // Difficulty combobox
36:     QStringList list = {"Easy", "Medium", "Hard"};
37:     ui->cmb_difficulty->addItems(list);
38:     int index = config->getDifficulty() - 1;
39:     qDebug() << "Difficulty index:" << index;
40:     ui->cmb_difficulty->setCurrentIndex(index);
41: 
42:     // Player color
43:     list = {"White", "Black"};
44:     ui->cmb_color->addItems(list);
45:     index = config->getColor() == true ? 0 : 1;
46:     qDebug() << "Color index:" << index;
47:     ui->cmb_color->setCurrentIndex(index);
48: 
49:     // Assisted mode
50:     list = {"On", "Off"};
51:     ui->cmb_assist->addItems(list);
52:     index = config->getAssistModeOn() == true ? 0 : 1;
53:     qDebug() << "Assist mode state:" << config->getAssistModeOn() << "Assisted mode:" << index;
54:     ui->cmb_assist->setCurrentIndex(index);
55: }
56:

59: {
60:     qDebug() << "Closing settings screen: Assist mode:" << config->getAssistModeOn() << "Color:" << config->getColor() << "Difficulty:" << config->getDifficulty();
61:     Q_EMIT settingsScreenClosed();
62:     this->close();
63: }

98:     config->setColor(isWhite);
99:     config->saveConfig();
100:     return;

105: {
106:     // Possible options {"Easy", "Medium", "Hard"};
107:     if (index == 0) {
108:         config->setDifficulty(1);
109:     } else if (index == 2) {
110:         config->setDifficulty(2);
111:     } else {
112:         config->setDifficulty(3);
113:     }
114: 
115:     config->saveConfig();
116:     return;

46: }

48: // Reopen this form (main menu) whenever a child form emits it's "I'm closing" signal
49: void StartScreen::on_childScreenClosed()
50: {
51:     config->refreshConfig();
52:     this->show();
53: }
54: 
55: // On pressing Play button, open a new instance of the game screen and hide the main menu
56: void StartScreen::on_btn_play_clicked()
57: {
58:     BoardScreen *boardScreen = new BoardScreen(this);
59:     boardScreen->setWindowState(Qt::WindowMaximized);
60:     boardScreen->show();
61: 
62:     connect(boardScreen, &BoardScreen::boardScreenClosed, this, &StartScreen::on_childScreenClosed);
63: 
64:     this->hide();
65: }
66: 
67: // On pressing Help button, open a new instance of the help screen and hide the main menu
68: void StartScreen::on_btn_help_clicked()
69: {
70:     HelpScreen *helpScreen = new HelpScreen(this);
71:     helpScreen->setWindowState(Qt::WindowMaximized);
72:     helpScreen->show();
73: 
74:     connect(helpScreen, &HelpScreen::helpScreenClosed, this, &StartScreen::on_childScreenClosed);
75: 
76:     this->hide();
77: }
78: 
79: // On pressing Settings button, open a new instance of the settings screen and hide the main menu
80: void StartScreen::on_btn_settings_clicked()
81: {
82:     SettingsScreen *settingsScreen = new SettingsScreen(this);
83:     settingsScreen->setWindowState(Qt::WindowMaximized);
84:     settingsScreen->show();
85: 
86:     connect(settingsScreen, &SettingsScreen::settingsScreenClosed, this, &StartScreen::on_childScreenClosed);
87: 
88:     this->hide();
89: }

File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/scripts\create_config.sql
1: -- Create table configuration
2: 
3: -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS public.configuration
4: 
5: CREATE TABLE configuration (
6:    config_id           	integer     SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
7:    config_difficulty 	integer     NOT NULL CHECK (config_difficulty >= 1) CHECK (config_difficulty <= 3),
8:    config_color 			boolean     NOT NULL,
9:    config_assist       	boolean     NOT NULL,
10: );
11: 
12: 
13: 
14: COMMENT ON TABLE configuration IS 'This table store persistent configuration settings';
15: COMMENT ON COLUMN configuration.config_id IS 'Unique identifier';
16: COMMENT ON COLUMN configuration.config_difficulty IS 'Difficulty; 1 - Easy, 2 - Medium, 3 - Hard';
17: COMMENT ON COLUMN configuration.config_color IS 'Player color; true - white, false - black';
18: COMMENT ON COLUMN configuration.config_assist IS 'Assist mode set; true - on, false - off';
19: 
20: -- End create table configuration

1: -- Create database game_metadata
2: 
3: -- DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS game_metadata;
4: 
5: CREATE DATABASE game_metadata
6:     WITH
7:     OWNER = postgres
8:     ENCODING = 'UTF8'
9:     LC_COLLATE = 'English_United States.1252'
10:     LC_CTYPE = 'English_United States.1252'
11:     LOCALE_PROVIDER = 'libc'
12:     TABLESPACE = pg_default
13:     CONNECTION LIMIT = -1
14:     IS_TEMPLATE = False;
15: 
16: -- End create database game_metadata


File: C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/scripts\create_table_metadata_game.sql
1: -- Create table metadata_game
2: 
3: -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS game_metadata.metadata_game
4: 
5: CREATE TABLE metadata_game (
6: 	game_id				integer		PRIMARY KEY,
7: 	game_player_color	integer		NOT NULL CHECK (game_player_color >= 0) CHECK (game_difficulty < 2),
8: 	game_winner_color	integer		NOT NULL CHECK (game_winner_color >= 0) CHECK (game_difficulty < 2),,
9: 	game_length			integer		NOT NULL,
10: 	game_moves			varchar(4000),
11: 	game_difficulty		integer		NOT NULL CHECK (game_difficulty >= 0) CHECK (game_difficulty < 4),
12: 	game_date			date		NOT NULL
13: );
14: 
15: 
16: 
17: COMMENT ON TABLE metadata_game IS 'This table stoes metadata about completed individual games';
18: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_id IS 'Unique game identifier';
19: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_player_color IS 'Players color; 0 - Black, 1 - White';
20: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_winner_color IS 'Winners color; 0 - Black, 1 - White';
21: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_length IS 'Length of game in minutes';
22: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_moves IS 'Algebraic notation of the moves completed';
23: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_difficulty IS 'Difficulty setting; 0 - Easy, 1 - Standard, 2 - Hard';
24: COMMENT ON COLUMN metadata_game.game_date IS 'Date played';
25: 
26: -- End create table metadata_game

9: #include "colorrepository.h"

11: #include <QApplication>
12: #include <QBrush>
13: #include <QToolTip>
14: 
15: template <class T>
16: constexpr const T &clamp(const T &v, const T &lo, const T &hi)
17: {
18:     return v < lo ? lo : hi < v ? hi : v;
19: }
20: 
21: static bool s_darkMode = true;
22: 
23: QPalette colorrepository::standardPalette()
24: {
25:     QPalette pal;
26:     pal.setColor(QPalette::Window, windowBackground());
27:     pal.setColor(QPalette::Base, baseBackground());
28:     pal.setColor(QPalette::WindowText, text());
29:     pal.setColor(QPalette::Text, text());
30: 
31:     // Text color on buttons
32:     pal.setColor(QPalette::ButtonText, text());
33: 
34:     // pal.setColor(QPalette::ToolTipBase, baseBackground());
35:     pal.setColor(QPalette::ToolTipText, text());
36: 
37:     QToolTip::setPalette(pal);
38: 
39:     return pal;
40: }
41: 
42: void colorrepository::setDarkMode(bool dark)
43: {
44:     s_darkMode = dark;
45:     qApp->setPalette(standardPalette());
46: }
47: 
48: QColor colorrepository::windowBackground()
49: {
50:     return s_darkMode ? QColor(0x18, 0x21, 0x29) // dark blue
51:                                     : QColor(0xef, 0xf0, 0xf1);
52: }
53: 
54: QColor colorrepository::baseBackground()
55: {
56:     return s_darkMode ? QColor(0x0f, 0x0f, 0x0f) // almost black
57:                                     : QColor(0xfb, 0xfb, 0xfb); // almost white
58: }
59: 
60: QColor colorrepository::text()
61: {
62:     return s_darkMode ? QColor(0xa5, 0xa5, 0xa5) : QColor(0x25, 0x25, 0x25);
63: }
64: 
65: QColor colorrepository::pressedTextColor()
66: {
67:     return QColor(0x65, 0x65, 0x65); // medium gray
68: }
69: 
70: QColor colorrepository::hoverTextColor()
71: {
72:     return QColor(0xdd, 0xdd, 0xdd); // light gray
73: }
74: 
75: QColor colorrepository::pressedOutlineColor()
76: {
77:     return QColor(0x32, 0x2d, 0x35);
78: }
79: 
80: QColor colorrepository::buttonOutlineColor()
81: {
82:     return s_darkMode ? QColor(0x59, 0x51, 0x5f) : QColor(0x9f, 0x95, 0xa3);
83: }
84: 
85: QBrush colorrepository::hoverOutlineBrush(const QRect &rect)
86: {
87:     // Instructions from the designer:
88:     // "Draw line passing by center of rectangle (+4% to the right)
89:     // and that is perpendicular to the topleft-bottomright diagonal.
90:     // This line intersects the top and bottom in two points, which are the gradient stops"
91: 
92:     const qreal w = rect.width();
93:     const qreal h = rect.height();
94:     const qreal xmid = w * 0.54;
95:     const qreal xoffset = (h * h) / (2 * w); // Proportionality: xoffset / (h/2) = h / w
96:     const qreal x0 = xmid - xoffset;
97:     const qreal x1 = xmid + xoffset;
98: 
99:     QLinearGradient gradient(x0, h, x1, 0);
100:     gradient.setColorAt(0.0, QColor(0x53, 0x94, 0x9f));
101:     gradient.setColorAt(1.0, QColor(0x75, 0x55, 0x79));
102:     return QBrush(gradient);
103: }
104: 
105: QColor colorrepository::buttonPressedBackground()
106: {
107:     return s_darkMode ? QColor(0x17, 0x17, 0x17) : QColor(0xf8, 0xf7, 0xf8);
108: }
109: 
110: QColor colorrepository::buttonHoveredBackground()
111: {
112:     QColor color = buttonPressedBackground();
113:     color.setAlphaF(0.2);
114:     return color;
115: }
116: 
117: QColor colorrepository::buttonBackground()
118: {
119:     return s_darkMode ? QColor(0x21, 0x1f, 0x22, 0xa7) : QColor(0xf5, 0xf4, 0xf5);
120: }
121: 
122: QBrush colorrepository::progressBarOutlineBrush(const QRect &rect)
123: {
124:     QLinearGradient gradient(0, rect.height(), rect.width(), 0);
125:     gradient.setColorAt(0.0, QColor(0x11, 0xc2, 0xe1));
126:     gradient.setColorAt(1.0, QColor(0x89, 0x3a, 0x94));
127:     return QBrush(gradient);
128: }
129: 
130: QBrush colorrepository::progressBarOutlineFadingBrush(const QRect &rect)
131: {
132:     QLinearGradient gradient(0, rect.height(), rect.width(), 0);
133:     gradient.setColorAt(0.0, QColor(0x11, 0xc2, 0xe1));
134:     gradient.setColorAt(1.0, QColor(0x89, 0x3a, 0x94));
135:     return QBrush(gradient);
136: }
137: 
138: QBrush colorrepository::progressBarContentsBrush(const QRect &rect)
139: {
140:     // same as outline brush but with 37% opacity
141:     QLinearGradient gradient(0, rect.height(), rect.width(), 0);
142:     gradient.setColorAt(0.0, QColor(0x11, 0xc2, 0xe1, 0x60));
143:     gradient.setColorAt(1.0, QColor(0x89, 0x3a, 0x94, 0x60));
144:     return QBrush(gradient);
145: }
146: 
147: QColor colorrepository::progressBarTextColor(bool enabled)
148: {
149:     QColor textColor = text();
150:     if (!enabled)
151:         textColor.setAlphaF(textColor.alphaF() / 2.0);
152:     return textColor;
153: }
